## AGY-1  (WS-DEPLOY, P1) — atomic+retried+verified for the remaining firstboot producers
**Who:** you (bash/systemd). **When:** first — it mirrors the webtools/venv fixes Claude already landed.
**What + How:** apply the 38-hermes-agent reference pattern to the producers that still "run once, give up":
- `usr/libexec/mios/mios-ai-firstboot` — the vLLM/GGUF weights fetch (the `snapshot_download` blocks, ~L111-124 + L371): wrap in a 3x retry-with-backoff loop, verify the target `config.json`/`.ready` exists after, non-fatal per-model, log clearly. (This is the code half of **T-178**; the heavy lane is skipped today purely because this fetch had no retry and ran through the then-missing venv.)
- `usr/libexec/mios/forge-firstboot.sh` — replace the fixed `300s` timeout abort with a **readiness poll** (poll the forge health/socket, generous cap, `Restart=on-failure` on the unit) so a slow forge under load never hard-fails.
- Any other `*-firstboot` producer with a bare one-shot build/fetch (grep `usr/libexec/mios/*firstboot*`).
**Where:** `usr/libexec/mios/mios-ai-firstboot`, `usr/libexec/mios/forge-firstboot.sh`, their `usr/lib/systemd/system/*.service` (`Restart=on-failure` + `StartLimit*`).
**Done When:** each producer is atomic+retried+verified+idempotent; `bash -n` clean; a fresh reinstall would deploy them without manual retries.

## AGY-2  (WS-DEPLOY, P1) — DAG-integrity drift-gate (consumer-before-producer = build error)
**Who:** you (bash + the drift-gate framework). **When:** after AGY-1.
**What + How:** add a new check to `automation/38-drift-checks.sh` (next free check number, currently 25-28 exist → add 29) that parses the producer→consumer map and FAILS when a consumer unit/step can start before its producer's readiness artifact exists — i.e. a consumer `.container`/`.service` that depends on a built image / seeded row / fetched model but lacks `After=`/`Requires=`/`ConditionPathExists=` on its producer. Follow the existing `check_*` function style in that file; wire it into `main`; keep it read-only + fast (no built image needed). Full spec: `usr/share/doc/mios/reference/install-ordering.md` (WS-DEPLOY).
**Where:** `automation/38-drift-checks.sh`.
**Done When:** the gate flags at least the known-good edges (webtools pod After webtools-firstboot; agent-pipe After the venv) and passes on the current tree; `just drift-gate` green.

## AGY-3  (WS-VECTOR V0, P1) — DB projection foundation (no behavior change)
**Who:** you (SQL + Python, no live DB needed — static SQL/codegen). **When:** independent; can start immediately.
**What + How:** lay the foundation for `everything-db-driven.md` V0 WITHOUT flipping any authority:
- `usr/share/mios/postgres/schema-init.sql` — add the `config_layer(rank,name)` precedence table (seed {0:vendor,1:host,2:user,3:machine}) and `config_kv(scope,key,value jsonb,layer FK,owner_user,description,emb vector(768),emb_model,emb_version)` with an HNSW index on `emb` (mirror the `knowledge`/`agent_memory` DDL exactly — same `vector_cosine_ops m=16 ef_construction=64`). Idempotent (`CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS` / guarded index).
- Write a **DB→TOML materialize** peer of `usr/libexec/mios/seed-db-config.py` (e.g. `usr/libexec/mios/materialize-config-toml.py`) that reads `config_kv`/`verb`/`domain_verb` and regenerates a TOML the drift-gate can diff — the inverse of today's TOML→DB seeding. Keep it read-only w.r.t. the DB.
- Make the existing `verb` round-trip **lossless**: ensure `seed-db-config.py` + the new materializer preserve section/examples/model_name/hidden/aliases/conflict_group/parallel_limit/max_result_chars.
**Where:** `usr/share/mios/postgres/schema-init.sql`, `usr/libexec/mios/seed-db-config.py`, new `usr/libexec/mios/materialize-config-toml.py`.
**Done When:** schema applies idempotently; `seed-db-config.py` TOML→DB then materialize DB→TOML round-trips a verb losslessly (diff clean); nothing reads the new tables at runtime yet (V1 flips that — leave it).

## AGY-5  (WS-GUARD / T-173, **P0**) — daemon runaway controls (host-pressure gate + dedup + cron cap)
**Who:** you (Python, agent-pipe/daemon). **When:** next — P0, prevents GPU/host runaway.
**What + How:** add guardrails to the consolidated micro-LLM daemon + agent-pipe so autonomous loops can't starve the host: (1) a **host-pressure gate** — before a heavy dispatch, check GPU VRAM / CPU load and defer/degrade to the light lane when over a threshold (from `[ai.host_thresholds]`); (2) **request dedup** — collapse identical in-flight prompts (hash the normalized messages) so a retry storm doesn't fan out N copies; (3) a **cron cap** — bound the daemon's scheduled classify/refusal jobs per interval. Degrade-open (missing signal → allow).
**Where:** `usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/**` (daemon/dispatch), `usr/libexec/mios/mios-daemon*`, `usr/share/mios/mios.toml` (`[ai.host_thresholds]`, a new `[ai.guard]` if needed).
**Done When:** a synthetic runaway (rapid identical heavy prompts under high VRAM) is gated/deduped, not fanned out; `test_mios_*` green.

**Who:** you (Python, agent-pipe). **When:** after AGY-5.

Budget target reads from SSOT; degrade-open if unset.

**Done When:** a fan-out that would blow the budget stops at the cap with a summary; a foreground request preempts a running background job; tests green.

## AGY-9  (WS-VECTOR V1 / T-243, **P1**) — config read-path resolver (kill the write-only `system_config` drift)
**Who:** you (Python). **When:** next — it's the payoff of your AGY-3 foundation (the tables exist and round-trip; now make something READ them).
**What + How:** write a DB config resolver that is a **peer of `mios_toml.py`**, reading `config_kv` / `verb` / `domain_verb` (the tables AGY-3 + `seed-db-config.py` populate) with the **baked `mios.toml` as fail-open fallback**. Contract: same 3-layer precedence semantics as the TOML overlay (vendor<host<user<machine via the `config_layer` rank), same return shapes the current `mios_toml.py` callers expect — a drop-in so a caller can flip its source with no behavior change. Add a **`[ai] db_authoritative` sentinel** (default **false**): when false, resolve from TOML exactly as today and only *shadow-compare* the DB answer (log divergence, count it); when true, resolve from DB with TOML fallback. This lets us flip authority per-surface later (V5) with the gate already watching. Do NOT flip any real caller yet — ship the resolver + shadow-compare + tests only.
**Where:** new `usr/lib/mios/mios_db_config.py` (peer of `usr/lib/mios/mios_toml.py`), `usr/share/mios/mios.toml` (`[ai] db_authoritative=false`), a `test_mios_db_config.py` under `usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/` (or `tests/`).
**Done When:** resolver returns identical values to `mios_toml.py` for a sampled set of keys/verbs (shadow-compare = 0 divergences on the current tree); TOML fail-open verified by pointing at an empty DB; `bash -n`/parse clean; tests green; `just drift-gate` passes. **Storage law:** vectors find, SQL reads — resolve from typed columns, never from `emb`.

## AGY-10  (WS-VECTOR V2 backfill / T-244, **P1**) — embed-backfill worker that actually FILLS your AGY-7 columns
**Who:** you (Python). **When:** after AGY-7 (you added the `emb` columns; nothing populates them yet — close the loop).
**What + How:** extend `mios_pipe/memory/embed_backfill.py` (or add a worker beside it) to populate the `emb vector(768)` columns AGY-7 added on `skill`/`verb`/`tool_call`/`directory_entry` by computing embeddings over each row's **TEXT PROJECTION** via `mios-llm-light /v1/embeddings` (`nomic-embed-text`, the same client seam `pg.py` uses). Must be: **idempotent** (only (re)embed rows whose `emb IS NULL` or whose `emb_version` is stale — never re-embed unchanged rows), **provenance-stamped** (`emb_model`/`emb_version` written with each vector), **batched with the 3x-retry-with-backoff pattern** (reference `38-hermes-agent.sh`), and **fail-open** (embeddings endpoint down → log + skip, never crash the caller). Then repoint the in-process verb/apps embedding rebuild (`worker_tools.py`) to prefer a native `verb.emb <=> query` lookup when populated, with the in-process lexicon as the fail-open fallback (this is the retirement AGY-7 set up).
**Where:** `usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/memory/embed_backfill.py`, `usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/routing/worker_tools.py`, a `test_mios_backfill.py`.
**Done When:** running the backfill on a seeded DB fills `verb.emb`/`skill.emb`/`tool_call.emb`/`directory_entry.emb` with provenance; a second run is a near-noop (idempotent); `<=>` verb search returns sane neighbors; endpoint-down path degrades to lexicon with no crash; tests green.

## AGY-25  (AUDIT FIXES, **P0/P1**) — resolve 10 defects a Claude adversarial audit CONFIRMED in your WS-VECTOR code
**Who:** you (Python + bash + SQL). **When:** NEXT — these are real, verified bugs in code you shipped (each independently code-traced + verified). Claude already fixed 2 (redact.py unquoted-secret leak + mios_db_config.py port fail-open) — do NOT redo those. Fix these 10:
**HIGH:**
1. **`verbcatalog.py` ~148-215 — the `db_authoritative` sentinel is a NO-OP.** The T-126 "Database Overlay" block runs UNCONDITIONALLY (only try/except-guarded), so with the sentinel FALSE (default) + pgvector up, the DB silently overlays/deletes verbs (`cat.pop` on is_active=false, overwrites sig/desc/tier/permission/cmd/params) — the returned catalog is NOT byte-identical to TOML. **Fix:** gate the entire T-126 overlay behind `is_db_authoritative()` so sentinel-FALSE returns the pure TOML catalog; keep only the shadow-compare (read-only) running when false.
2. **`embed_backfill.py` ~209-248 + `toolsearch.py` ~206-231 — emb_version PING-PONG on `verb`.** Backfill stamps `emb_version='nomic-768-v1'`; toolsearch treats a verb vector valid only if `emb_version == <sha256 fp>` and re-stamps fp. The two writers perpetually invalidate each other -> every core/common verb re-embeds every 15-min timer run (never idempotent). **Fix:** unify to ONE scheme on `verb.emb_version` (make backfill compute+store the SAME fingerprint toolsearch uses, OR make toolsearch honor backfill's version) so a stamped vector satisfies both readers.
3. **`agent_call.py` ~93/436/543 — token guard permanently WEDGES a session.** `_SESSION_TOKENS[session_id]` is cumulative-only, never windowed/reset; once a session crosses `conversation_token_ceil` (2M) `used > conv_ceil` raises `ValueError` on EVERY later dispatch for the process lifetime -> the user can never get another answer until daemon restart. **Fix:** make it a rolling window + graceful summarize (mirror `chat.py`'s `_budget_admit`/`_BUDGET_LEDGER`), not a permanent hard-raise.
**MEDIUM:**
4. **`mios_db_config.py` ~13/197 — `DIVERGENCES` counts read-observations, never resets** -> the health `config_divergences` gauge climbs unbounded on any persistent mismatch read on hot paths. **Fix:** track a SET of distinct divergent `scope.key`s (or reset per rebuild) so the gauge = number of divergent settings.
5. **`verbcatalog.py` ~234 — shadow-compare feeds the ALREADY-DB-OVERLAID `cat`** into `_compare_catalogs`, masking real TOML-vs-DB drift on shared verbs AND firing a false divergence for every TOML-only verb during partial migration. **Fix:** snapshot a PRE-overlay pure-TOML copy and compare THAT vs `db_cat`.
**LOW:**
6. `verbcatalog.py` ~225 — redundant SECOND blocking `psycopg.connect(connect_timeout=2)` on the sentinel-FALSE path (~4s dead wait when DB down). Skip/cache when not db_authoritative.
7. `toolsearch.py` ~231 — stamps `emb_model='qwen2.5-coder:1.5b'` on nomic-produced verb vectors (false provenance, disagrees with backfill's `nomic-embed-text`). Stamp the actual embed model.
8. `embed_backfill.py` ~243-249 — `embedded_count += 1` runs even when the degrade-open `mios_pg.execute()` UPDATE returned None (silent DB failure over-reported as success). Check the return; count only real writes.
9. `automation/38-drift-checks.sh` check 32 (~2707-2770) — "lossless" round-trip only diffs pkgs + phase ordinal/deps/stage; add `enable`/`layer`/`base_image_ref`/`section` + `debloat_profile.description` + `preset.debloat_profile_name` to the diff.
10. `materialize-build-ctx.py` ~59 — same-ordinal `build_phase` tie-breaks by DB `id`, so an incremental re-seed sorts a new same-prefix script after older peers instead of lexically. **Fix:** `ORDER BY stage, ordinal NULLS LAST, script` (lexical), not `id`.
**Where/Done When:** fix each at the cited file:line; add/extend tests (`test_mios_db_config`/`test_mios_backfill`/`test_mios_verbcatalog`) to cover the fixed behavior; `just drift-gate` green; **stage only your files (never the Quadlets).**

## AGY-27  (embedding hygiene / research-gap #6+#7, **P1**) — fix the emb_version space-collision + add EmbeddingGemma task prefixes
**Who:** you (Python + SQL). **When:** NEXT after AGY-25 — this OVERLAPS AGY-25 finding #2 (unify the emb_version scheme first). Source: gaps 6+7.
**What + How:** two real embedding-correctness bugs: (a) the served embedding model was swapped **nomic-embed-text → EmbeddingGemma-300m under the SAME served name AND same emb_version**, so two incompatible 768-d vector spaces now collide in one namespace — **bump the emb_version** (a new fingerprint that includes the actual model+revision) so old-space vectors are treated stale and re-embedded, and make backfill + toolsearch agree on that ONE fingerprint (this IS the AGY-25 #2 unification — do them together). (b) EmbeddingGemma REQUIRES task prompt templates (`task: search result | query: …` / document prefixes) — the embed call path (`server.py` embed seam + `embed_backfill.py`) sends **raw text**, degrading recall. Add the EmbeddingGemma query/document prefixes at the embed seam (gated by the active embed model so nomic-only setups are unaffected). Then trigger a one-time full re-embed via the backfill worker.
**Where:** `usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/memory/embed_backfill.py` + `routing/toolsearch.py` (emb_version unify), the embed seam in `server.py`, `usr/share/mios/mios.toml` (embed model/version), `test_mios_backfill.py`.
**Done When:** old-space vectors are invalidated + re-embedded once (not ping-ponging — see AGY-25 #2); EmbeddingGemma requests carry the task prefixes; nomic path unchanged; recall verified sane; tests + `just drift-gate` green.

## AGY-28  (AGY-25 RESIDUALS, **P1**) — close the 4 residual defects a Claude verification pass found still open after AGY-25
**Who:** you (Python). **When:** NEXT. A Claude adversarial re-verify confirmed AGY-25 landed 10/10 but left these tails:
1. **`agent_call.py` — D3 still HARD-RAISES.** The rolling-window is in (good, permanent-wedge gone) but once the 1h-windowed total exceeds `conversation_token_ceil` it still raises `ValueError` (500-style) instead of the **graceful summarize** the defect asked for. **Fix:** mirror `chat.py`'s `_budget_admit` degrade — summarize/trim + admit, never a hard raise on a live session.
2. **`mios_db_config.py` + `verbcatalog.py:~246` — D4 not airtight.** `get_divergences()` sums the deduped `_DIVERGENT_KEYS` set PLUS the raw int `DIVERGENCES`, and `verbcatalog.py` still does `mios_db_config.DIVERGENCES += 1` per divergent reload. **Fix:** route the verbcatalog contributor into the SAME `_DIVERGENT_KEYS` set (scope.key granularity) and drop the raw-int path so the gauge = distinct divergent settings.
3. **`embed_backfill.py` — D2 co-residency assumption.** `_verb_embed_fingerprint()` reads toolsearch's module-global `_VERB_CATALOG`; if the 15-min worker runs in a process where `configure()` never populated it, the fp is computed over an empty catalog → churn returns. **Fix:** guard/assert the catalog is populated before fingerprinting (skip the run + log if empty), or compute the fp from the same SSOT source both processes read.
4. **`verbcatalog.py` — D6 first-load blocking connect.** On the sentinel-FALSE path the FIRST load still does one blocking `psycopg.connect(connect_timeout=2)` before `_DB_UNREACHABLE` caches. **Fix:** short-circuit the very first probe too (cache the unreachable state across the initial call, or make the probe non-blocking/background).
**Done When:** each fixed at cited file:line; tests extended; `just drift-gate` green; stage only your files.

## AGY-29  (WS-VECTOR V4 hardening / T-246, **P2**) — fix the two AGY-22/23 residuals a Claude verify pass flagged

## AGY-33  (audit-redaction depth / follow AGY-32, **P2**) — make config_event redaction VALUE-aware, not just scope/key-aware
**Who:** you (SQL + Python test). **When:** after AGY-32. The Day-0 readiness audit found a coverage gap in the `mios_redact_config_value()` fix (Claude commit 3abc92f): `seed-db-config.py` §1c seeds the `[containers]` scope into config_kv, whose Environment arrays embed secrets — `K3S_TOKEN=...` (mios.toml:10004), `WEBUI_SECRET_KEY=...` (:10183), `POSTGRES_PASSWORD`/`SUDO_PASSWORD`/`PASSWORD` (9717-18, 10264). The trigger only redacts when `scope IN ('security','agent_passport')` OR the IMMEDIATE key matches the secret regex; `scope='containers', key='mios-k3s'` matches neither, so the whole container JSON (secrets included) lands in config_event verbatim. Same structural miss for any secret nested in a subtable of a non-secret scope.
**How (pick one, document why):** (a) make `mios_redact_config_value` recurse the JSONB value and mask (i) any object key matching the secret regex and (ii) any string of the `NAME=VALUE` env-array shape where NAME matches the regex; OR (b) exclude `scope IN ('containers','image')` from the config_kv seed loop in seed-db-config.py (they're Quadlet-shaped, not operator config — also trims audit noise). Extend `test_mios_config_audit` (your AGY-32 test) to seed a container row with an env secret and assert the config_event new_value is masked.
**Done When:** no container/nested secret reaches config_event in plaintext; test proves it; `just drift-gate` green. Do NOT touch Claude's schema-init trigger signature without keeping the `mios_redact_config_value(scope,key,value)` contract.

## AGY-34  (Quadlet-reconciler hygiene / from readiness audit, **P3**) — fix the mios-llm-heavy-alt dead drop-in wiring
**Who:** you (bash + Quadlet). **When:** parallel-safe; coordinate with AGY-31 (same etc/containers space). The readiness audit (LOW) found `MIOS_AI_QUADLETS_DEFAULT` in `usr/libexec/mios/mios-gpu-passthrough:85` lists `mios-llm-heavy-alt`, and the tree ships `etc/containers/systemd/mios-llm-heavy-alt.container.d/20-mios-igpu.conf`, but there is NO base `mios-llm-heavy-alt.container` under `usr/share/containers/systemd` (only `mios-llm-heavy.container`). ## AGY-36  (INSTALL HARDENING: service resilience + log-spam, **P1**) — AI services must degrade-open QUIETLY, not flood the journal
**Who:** you (Python + systemd). **When:** NOW. Operator feedback from the live reinstall: "TOO MANY OUTAGES, not hardened." Root observed: when `mios-llm-light` (the embed backend) is down (no GGUFs), `mios-agent-pipe` + hermes flood the journal with `WARNING embed call failed: All connection attempts failed` (hundreds of lines in ms) yet DO serve (0-embedding degrade-open). **Fix:** (1) in the embed call path (`mios_pipe/**` toolsearch/embed seam), rate-limit/dedupe the failure log — log ONCE + exponential backoff, not per-verb-per-call; the service must stay up + serve `:8640`/`:8642` with 0 embeddings and RE-embed automatically once llm-light comes up (poll/backoff, no restart needed). (2) Audit EVERY `usr/share/containers/systemd/mios-*.container` + `usr/lib/systemd/system/mios-*.service` for `Restart=on-failure` + `RestartSec` + correct `After=`/`Wants=` so a service self-heals when its dependency later appears (no operator re-deploy). Report any AI-plane unit missing Restart=.
**Done When:** no journal flood when llm-light is down; agent-pipe/hermes stay `active` + HTTP 200 on `/v1/models`; embeddings backfill automatically when llm-light returns; every AI unit has a restart policy; `just drift-gate` green.

## AGY-41  (WS-DEBT / TD-1 / T-269, **P0 security**) — eliminate the `eval`-on-agent-args injection surface in the verb library
**Who:** you (bash). **When:** the eval-fixes NOW (disjoint); the guard-check after Claude's push. Do NOT touch `mios-theme-render` (Claude-staged).
**What + How:** the tech-debt audit found **~9 runtime verbs in `usr/libexec/mios/` that `eval` agent-derived arguments** — a command-injection surface (a tool/agent controlling a verb arg can execute arbitrary shell). (1) `grep -rn 'eval ' usr/libexec/mios/` to enumerate the exact set; (2) replace each `eval` with a safe form — quoted arg arrays (`"$@"`), a `case` allowlist dispatch, or `printf %q` — so agent-supplied values can never be re-parsed as shell; (3) for any `eval` that is genuinely load-bearing with **no** agent-controlled input (verify provenance), leave it with a `# TD-1: eval-safe, input=<source>, not agent-controlled` justification rather than a blind rewrite (per the flatten "don't blind-delete load-bearing" caution). Then add a **drift-check** to `38-drift-checks.sh` that FAILS if a NEW `eval` on a `$MIOS_*`/argv value appears under `usr/libexec/mios/`.
**Where:** the ~9 `eval` verbs under `usr/libexec/mios/`, `automation/38-drift-checks.sh` (the guard — after Claude's push, per the gate).
**Done When:** no verb `eval`s an agent-controlled value; each remaining `eval` is justified input-safe; the injection-guard drift-check is green on HEAD and reds an injected `eval "$MIOS_FOO"`; `bash -n` clean; `just drift-gate` green.

**What + How:** the Portal already embeds the configurator (`GET /portal/configurator` serves mios.html into the shell iframe), but mios.html can only save via browser download — there is NO server read/write of the SSOT. Add two routes:
- **`GET /portal/config`** → return the live LAYERED `mios.toml` (vendor<host<user) as `text/plain` TOML for the form to seed from. Reuse the existing read path (the `tomllib.load` the Portal already does for `[colors]`/`[ports]`, `mios_pipe/kernel/config.py`).
- **`POST /portal/config`** → body = raw TOML; validate it parses; PERSIST to the **user layer `~/.config/mios/mios.toml`** by default (host `/etc/mios/mios.toml` only when the session is a privileged/admin operator). Return a JSON status. **Persist-only — do NOT trigger `mios build`** (apply stays an explicit operator action).
- Add the **writer** to `mios_pipe/kernel/config.py` (currently read-only): write the correct layer file atomically (temp+rename), preserving SSOT cascade semantics.
- **Auth:** reuse the portal session (`_portal_authed`) + honor `[security].api_require_auth`; when unauthorized/disabled return 403/404 so the client gracefully falls back to browser-download (the client half is built to degrade).
- Wire the routes in `mios_pipe/routing/portal.py` + the thin `@app`/router entry in `server.py` (coordinate with your AGY-47 decomposition).
**Where:** `usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/kernel/config.py` (writer), `usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/routing/portal.py` (routes), `usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/server.py` (wiring), a `test_mios_config_write.py`.
**Done When:** `GET /portal/config` returns the live TOML; `POST /portal/config` persists to `~/.config/mios/mios.toml` atomically, auth-gated, no build triggered; unauthorized → 403 so the client degrades to download; tests green; `just drift-gate` green. Stage only your files.
**OPEN (operator may adjust):** the write-layer default (per-user vs host), and whether a future 'Apply' action should trigger `mios build` (out of scope here — persist-only for now).

## AGY-57..58 — ADR-0010 completion (from a Claude design workflow: extend mios-theme-render IN PLACE, NO mios-dotfiles-render fork)

> These implement the `kind` axis + merge modes for the dotfiles engine Claude built (`_load_surfaces`/`_KINDS`/cmd_render/cmd_check/cmd_apply in `usr/libexec/mios/mios-theme-render`). CORE RULE: `kind` is WRITE-SEMANTICS dispatch, ORTHOGONAL to the existing `section` (token-source). ABSENT `kind` ⇒ `template` ⇒ the 8 existing surfaces need ZERO edits + stay BYTE-IDENTICAL. Preserve every fail-loud backstop (unknown kind ⇒ `exit 3`; a merge surface missing its fixture ⇒ `exit 3`). `capture` stays template-only.

## AGY-57  (WS-DOTFILES / ADR-0010, **P2**) — the `kind` axis + `json-merge` mode (Windows Terminal / VS Code settings.json)
> **[DONE by Claude on main -- ea756065] kind axis + json-merge landed; verified check PASS 9, foreign-key-preserving, fail-loud exit 3.**
**Who:** you (Python). **When:** first of the two; parallel-safe (mios-theme-render is Claude-owned but idle).
**What + How:**
1. **kind axis:** add optional `kind` to `[dotfiles.registry.<surface>]` ∈ `template|json-merge|ini-merge|registry|skip` (absent ⇒ `template`). `_load_surfaces` (~L46) returns a namedtuple `_Surface(name,template,target,section,kind,fixture,policy)` (so `_entry`/template call sites are untouched); it VALIDATES: unknown kind ⇒ `exit 3` (same posture as the missing-template `exit 3` at L64-67); a merge kind MUST declare `fixture.base` + `fixture.expected` else `exit 3` (no ungated merge surface — preserves the no-vacuous-green stance).
2. **dispatch:** module-level `_KINDS = {kind: (derive_fn, live_apply_fn)}`. `cmd_render`/`cmd_check` select `derive_fn` by `surface.kind` and keep the uniform shape `derive(surface,merged)->committed_target_bytes` then write/byte-diff (check NEVER reads a live foreign file — offline PR gate). `cmd_apply` selects `live_apply_fn`. template kind = today's `_render_text` whole-file (cmd_apply L343-393 UNCHANGED).
3. **json-merge derive/apply:** `owned = _render_text(tmpl, _resolved_for(merged,section))` is a MiOS-owned JSON SUBTREE (only the keys MiOS projects — e.g. VS Code `workbench.colorCustomizations` or WT `profiles.defaults`/`schemes[]`). `derive = json_merge(owned, fixture.base)`; `apply = json_merge(owned, LIVE dest) -> write-back + backup`. `json_merge`: (a) `_jsonc_to_json(base)` — a STRING-AWARE comment/trailing-comma strip that never mangles `https://` or a `//` inside a string value; if base won't parse ⇒ `exit 2`, write NOTHING (never corrupt an unreadable file). (b) `json.loads` (insertion-ordered). (c) deep-merge: recurse dicts; a MiOS-owned leaf/array wins (arrays REPLACED wholesale at the owned pointer — index-merge is unsafe); any key MiOS does NOT emit is byte-preserved. (d) `json.dump` with base indent, `ensure_ascii=False`.
4. **drift-gating for merge surfaces:** the surface declares `fixture.base` (a checked-in canonical base) + `fixture.expected` (the expected merged output); `check` = `derive(owned, fixture.base)` byte-diff `fixture.expected`. Add a proof `json-merge` surface (e.g. `vscode-colors`: a small MiOS-owned colorCustomizations template + a `fixture.base` that already contains a FOREIGN key + the `fixture.expected` with that foreign key preserved).
**Where:** `usr/libexec/mios/mios-theme-render` (`_load_surfaces`, `_KINDS`, `_jsonc_to_json`/`_json_deep_merge`, cmd_render/check/apply branch), `usr/share/mios/mios.toml` (the new surface + `kind`/`fixture`), a new `.tmpl`, a fixtures dir (e.g. `usr/share/mios/theme/fixtures/`).
**Done When:** the 8 existing surfaces render/check **byte-identical** (kind defaults template — prove with the render byte-diff); the `json-merge` proof surface merges owned keys into `fixture.base` PRESERVING the foreign key (test); `check` gates it via the fixture; `apply` into a live temp target preserves foreign + writes a backup; unknown-kind / missing-fixture ⇒ `exit 3`; unparseable base ⇒ `exit 2` no-write; `capture` still template-only; `just drift-gate` green. Stage only your files.

## AGY-58  (WS-DOTFILES / ADR-0010, **P2**) — `ini-merge` mode + a `gitconfig-live` surface (UNBLOCK gitconfig live-apply)
> **[DONE by Claude on main -- 8f52ccfb] ini-merge + gitconfig-live landed; check PASS 10, live-apply preserves credential/signing/remotes + seeds owned + backup. gitconfig live-apply UNBLOCKED.**
**Who:** you (Python). **When:** after AGY-57 (needs the `kind` dispatch + `_KINDS`).
**What + How:**
1. **ini-merge derive/apply:** `_parse_ini(text)` keeps an ORDERED line-model + a `{(section,subsection,key)->line_idx}` index (preserves `#`/`;` comments + `[section "subsection"]` quoting). `owned_kv = _parse_ini(_render_text(gitconfig.tmpl))` — so MiOS owns EXACTLY the keys the template emits (`user.name/email`, `core.editor`, `init.defaultBranch`, `pull.rebase`, `alias.{co,br,ci,st}`). `_ini_upsert` per owned key: ABSENT in base ⇒ seed (append the section block if the section is absent); PRESENT ⇒ replace value in place per policy. Everything NOT in `owned_kv` (`credential`, `user.signingkey`, `commit.gpgsign`, remotes) is byte-preserved. Subsectioned keys keyed on `(section,subsection)` so they never collide; leave foreign multivar keys untouched (owned set is single-valued).
2. **merge write policy** `seed-or-enforce` (default for gitconfig, safety-first): per owned key — ABSENT ⇒ write (seed); PRESENT + `operator_set(key)` ⇒ write (enforce the operator's explicit SSOT choice); PRESENT + NOT `operator_set` ⇒ SKIP (never stomp an existing foreign value with a vendor default). `operator_set = mios_toml.load_merged(sec,key) != mios_toml.load_vendor(sec,key)` AND non-empty.
3. **gitconfig-live surface (NEW, ADDITIVE):** `kind=ini-merge`, `policy=seed-or-enforce`, `template` REUSES `usr/share/mios/theme/templates/gitconfig.tmpl` VERBATIM (the rendered template's `[section] key=value` lines ARE the ownership manifest AND the values), `apply.target.linux="~/.gitconfig"`, `apply.target.windows="%USERPROFILE%/.gitconfig"`, `fixture.base`/`fixture.expected` = a small canonical gitconfig pair. The EXISTING `gitconfig` surface (etc/skel/.gitconfig, kind=template, NO apply.target) stays BYTE-IDENTICAL. This is the safe unblock of the live-apply Claude withheld (whole-file overwrite would clobber the user credential/signing/remotes; ini-merge sets only the ~9 owned keys).
**Where:** `usr/libexec/mios/mios-theme-render` (`_parse_ini`/`_ini_upsert`/`_operator_set` + the ini-merge `_KINDS` entry), `usr/share/mios/mios.toml` (the `gitconfig-live` surface), a fixtures pair.
**Done When:** the existing `gitconfig` (template) surface is byte-identical; `apply gitconfig-live` into a live `~/.gitconfig` seeded with a FOREIGN `[credential]`/`user.signingkey`/remote PRESERVES them (assert) while setting the owned keys; `seed-or-enforce` SKIPS an existing foreign `user.email` unless operator_set; `check` gates via the fixture; a backup is written on change; unknown/missing-fixture ⇒ `exit 3`; `just drift-gate` green. Stage only your files.

## AGY-59  (WS-DOTFILES / ADR-0010, **P2**) — the `registry` kind (Windows Registry apply) + a windows-registry proof surface
**Who:** you (Python + PowerShell). **When:** after AGY-57/58 (landed).
**What + How:** add `registry` to `_KINDS`. Semantics (per the design): `derive` = build a manifest of the MiOS-owned Registry values (from `_render_text(tmpl,...)` -> a small JSON/INI-ish manifest of `HKCU\Path\Name = value` entries), byte-diffed against `fixture.expected` for the offline gate (check NEVER touches the live Registry). `live_apply_fn` = **Linux/non-Windows: no-op SKIP** (log "registry surface -- Windows-only, skipping"); **Windows (`os.name=='nt'`)**: apply each owned value via `reg add`/PowerShell `Set-ItemProperty` under HKCU only (refuse HKLM/system hives), reading back to confirm; back up the prior values first (export the owned keys to a `.mios-bak` .reg). Fail-loud: a registry surface missing `fixture.base/expected` => exit 3 (same as other merge kinds). ### AGY-84 REFINEMENT (Claude, VERIFIED against HEAD 3551d6d5) -- do NOT naive-emit ~500 vars
The drift-check "referenced but NOT emitted (a consumer would lose its var)" is OVER-BROAD. I read two representatives and confirmed the premise is false for the bulk:
- `server.py:804` `MIOS_ACI_HEAD_FRAC` = `_cfg_num(_ACI_TOML,"MIOS_ACI_HEAD_FRAC","head_frac",0.6,float)` -> reads `[aci].head_frac` from mios.toml SSOT with default; env is an OPTIONAL override. Consumer canNOT lose its var.
- `test_mios_template.py:48` `MIOS_NONEXISTENT_ENV` = deliberate test sentinel ("default absent -> fallback"). Must NEVER be emitted.
**Fix the CHECK to its true intent (flag only a var a consumer would GENUINELY lose), by category:**
- **A. SSOT-section reads (bulk):** `_cfg_num`/`_cfg_bool`/`_cfg_str`/`_toml_section(...)` with an env-name arg AND a default -> COMPLIANT (var IS SSOT-sourced). Recognize these; do not flag. This is most of server.py / mios_pipe/**/config.py / kernel.
- **B. test/negative sentinels:** anything referenced ONLY under `test_*.py`, `tests/`, `*-negatives.sh`, or the `38-ssot-lint.sh` fixtures (MIOS_NONEXISTENT_ENV, MIOS_NO_SUCH_VAR_XYZ, MIOS_FOO, MIOS_FIXTURE_*, MIOS_AI_TEST_TEMP, MIOS_BENCH, MIOS_EGRESS_TOOL, MIOS_MTLS_TOOL, MIOS_AUTONOMOUS_PRIORITY, MIOS_ANSWER_CHUNK_CHARS...) -> EXCLUDE from the scan.
- **C. regex prefix fragments:** trailing `_` or `__` captures (MIOS_A2O_, MIOS_AGENT_, MIOS_PORT_, MIOS_NATIVE_LOOP_, MIOS_DRIVE__, MIOS_COLS__, MIOS_CELL_H__ ...) -> tighten the extraction regex so it does NOT capture partial identifiers / `${MIOS_x_}${suffix}` interpolation stems.
- **D. Windows PowerShell vars:** any hit in `*.ps1` (Get-MiOS.ps1, build-mios.ps1, mios-pipeline.ps1) is a WinPS var -> NOT a Linux env key; userenv.sh (bash) neither can nor should emit it. Route to the PS globals.ps1 SSOT lane; EXCLUDE `.ps1` from the "must be emitted by userenv.sh" scan.
- **E. genuine residue:** after A-D, the SMALL set of real bash/systemd consumers that read `${MIOS_X}` with NO default and NO SSOT-section read -> THESE emit from the auto-derived key library (WS-NAME), sourced from mios.toml, reconciling MIOS_AI_VLLM_* <-> short MIOS_VLLM_*.
**Done (unchanged):** 0 GENUINE referenced-but-not-emitted; A-D no longer flagged; twins identical (drift-27); add a negative test PER category (a Cat-A `_cfg_num` var, a Cat-B sentinel, a Cat-D `.ps1` var) proving they're correctly NOT flagged, and one Cat-E var proving a real orphan IS flagged until emitted.

## AGY-89  (WS-RELTOP hardening, **P1**) -- globals.sh clobbers the SSOT image name (audit-confirmed)
**Who:** you (your WS-RELTOP/T-252 code). An independent audit found your credential-driven selection has a real latent bug + a misleading framing:
- **Bug (E1):** `automation/lib/globals.sh:109-113` -- the no-creds branch does `export MIOS_IMAGE_NAME="localhost/mios"` UNCONDITIONALLY. `common.sh` sources `userenv.sh` FIRST (ghcr from SSOT) then `globals.sh`, so on a no-creds host this OVERWRITES userenv's ghcr with localhost -- contradicting your own `common.sh:48-52` comment ("globals fills gaps") and the "userenv stays faithful to SSOT" claim. It also leaves `MIOS_IMAGE_NAME=localhost/mios` while `MIOS_IMAGE_REF` stays ghcr (`:=` at :116) -> an inconsistent name/ref pair. Harmless TODAY only because no reachable consumer pulls via `$MIOS_IMAGE_NAME` (consumers are display/legacy/CI-sources-userenv-directly) -- but a landmine: any future `bootc switch`/`podman pull "$MIOS_IMAGE_NAME"` after `common.sh` on a no-cred host -> `localhost/mios` -> crash.
- **Framing:** the real build path (`usr/libexec/mios/mios-build-driver:766`) HARDCODES `localhost/mios:latest` and never sources globals; the fresh Windows/Linux entry points never source globals either -> the credential-selection block is effectively dead on all fresh paths.
**Fix:** replace the whole `_has_registry_creds` if/else (`globals.sh:~101-113`) with a non-clobbering default: `: "${MIOS_IMAGE_NAME:=ghcr.io/mios-dev/mios}"` (MIOS_LOCAL_IMAGE already carries the localhost tag; keep credential gating only on a build-vs-publish DECISION, never on the image NAME).
- **E4 (twin parity):** `automation/lib/globals.ps1:62-92` respects `$env:MIOS_IMAGE_NAME` in BOTH branches while `globals.sh` forces localhost in the no-creds branch -> the two "SSOT" twins disagree on override semantics. Align them (both = non-clobbering `:=` default to ghcr, local tag via MIOS_LOCAL_IMAGE).
**Done:** no-creds host keeps `MIOS_IMAGE_NAME=ghcr.io/mios-dev/mios` (name/ref consistent); sh+ps1 twins equivalent; drift-gate (41/45 resolver-twin) stays green; add a negative test asserting a no-creds `common.sh` load does NOT downgrade MIOS_IMAGE_NAME to localhost.

## AGY-92  (audit BLOCKERS, **P0** -- deploy/user-facing breakage that ships GREEN gates) -- fix FIRST
An adversarial audit vetted 8 of your workstreams (ALL needs-refinement). Claude spot-verified B2+B4 directly. Each ships a GREEN drift-gate because a fixture/generator encodes the wrong behavior -> the gate cannot catch it.

**B1 (WS-BLADE -- deploy-time bootc failure):** the MIOSSYS refactor (c47ed570) moved bakes to `57-mios-sys-build.sh` + `mios-bake-group extra`, but `automation/08-system-files-overlay.sh:173-184` still `ln -sf`'s EVERY `.image` quadlet into `/usr/lib/bootc/bound-images.d/`. `mios-llm-heavy-alt.image` (sglang, group sys) + `mios-llama-swap.image` (llama-swap, group cuda) are now in NO baked group -> `57` builds localhost/mios-sys + localhost/mios-cuda via `COPY --from` but never pulls those engines into $STORE as resolvable bound refs -> `bootc` "does not resolve to an image ID" at INSTALL. **Fix:** re-add a `mios-bake-group sys` + `mios-bake-group cuda` RUN (per the [build.bake] "one RUN per group" comment) OR retire the two bound `.image` quadlets so 08-overlay stops binding them. Add a build-time assertion that every bound-images.d symlink resolves.

**B2 (WS-CONFIG -- Save DOA; VERIFIED by Claude):** `usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/kernel/config.py:537-549` range-checks every `[ports].*` as 1..65535, but `mios.toml:7775 [ports].stack_id = 0` is a port-OFFSET MULTIPLIER, not a port. `validate_config(full-toml)` -> ok=False "[ports].stack_id = 0 is out of the valid 1-65535 range"; omitting [ports] trips the "Refusing to drop critical [ports]" guard (:527). The configurator POSTs full TOML -> **422 for every operator, zero edits**. **Fix:** exempt non-listening keys (denylist `stack_id`, or only range-check keys that resolve to a real listening port). Add a round-trip test over the committed mios.toml.

**B3 (ADR-0010 -- breaks ALL ssh):** the dotfiles surface reuses `kind="ini-merge"` (git-config INI parser) for OpenSSH `ssh-config` -> emits `[host "mios-*"]` bracketed headers with `=`, which OpenSSH rejects (`Bad configuration option`). `mios.toml` maps apply.target -> `~/.ssh/config`, so `mios-dotfiles-render apply ssh-config` writes an unparseable file. Gate is green only because `fixtures/ssh-config.expected` encodes the SAME wrong format. **Fix:** add a dedicated ssh-config kind (or plain-template surface) emitting real stanza syntax (`Host mios-*` + tab-indented keywords, NO brackets/`=`); regenerate `.base`/`.expected`.

**B4 (liquid-glass -- work is DEAD; VERIFIED by Claude):** `automation/54-bake-hyprland.sh:13` does `cat << 'EOF' > /usr/share/mios/hyprland/hyprland.conf` -- the build UNCONDITIONALLY regenerates the file from the inline heredoc (still rounding=10/passes=3, no vibrancy/liquid beziers), DISCARDING every edit to the tracked artifact. **Fix:** apply the liquid-glass + spring-curve changes to the heredoc INSIDE 54-bake-hyprland.sh (the real source), preserving the `@@MIOS_COLOR_*@@` placeholders + Cockpit windowrules/`$mainMod, C` keybind; then delete/gitignore the tracked artifact OR add a drift-check asserting artifact == generator output.

**H1 (CI publish -- empty image name):** `.github/workflows/mios-ci.yml:308` sources userenv but never sets MIOS_VENDOR_TOML -> on stock ubuntu runners MIOS_IMAGE_NAME is UNSET -> malformed `:latest` tags + `podman login ''`; PUBLISH=true (:38) so NOT gated on GitHub. **Fix:** `export MIOS_VENDOR_TOML="$GITHUB_WORKSPACE/mios.toml"` before sourcing, or `: "${MIOS_IMAGE_NAME:=${REGISTRY}/${IMAGE_NAME}}"`.

## AGY-96  (WS-HARDEN / build-net, **P1**) — curl-retry drift-gate [DONE] ✔
**Who:** you (bash + drift-gate). **When:** FIRST — highest leverage; a ~20h publish loss traced to ONE retry-less `curl`.
**What + How:** the build died repeatedly on a transient GitHub `504` because `usr/share/mios/sys/Containerfile`'s AdGuard `RUN curl … | tar` had no `--retry`. Claude hand-swept every fetch; now ENFORCE it. Add a check to `automation/38-drift-checks.sh` (next free number) that greps every build-time network fetch and FAILS on any lacking a retry flag:
- `RUN … curl …` / bare `curl … http(s)://` across all `**/Containerfile` (sys, agents, cuda), `automation/*.sh`, `automation/lib/*.sh`, `usr/libexec/mios/*.sh`, `automation/90-generate-sbom.sh`.
- COMPLIANT iff it carries `--retry` OR routes through `scurl` (which injects retry) OR is explicitly listed in a `mios.toml [build.net].retry_exempt` allowlist (document each exemption).
- Recognize `wget` (`--tries`) too. Read-only, fast, no built image.
**Where:** `automation/38-drift-checks.sh`, `usr/share/mios/mios.toml` (`[build.net].retry_exempt` if needed).
**Done When:** the gate flags an injected retry-less `curl`, passes clean on HEAD (all fetches now retried), + a negative test proving the injected case is caught; `just drift-gate` green.

## AGY-97  (WS-HARDEN / scurl correctness, **P1**) — fix the scurl binary-stream corruption + harden its arg-parser
**Who:** you (bash). **When:** next — this is a real DATA-CORRUPTION bug, not just hygiene.
**What + How:** `automation/lib/masking.sh` `scurl()` sets `is_binary` ONLY when it sees `-o/-O/--output`. But the build's dominant pattern is `curl … | tar` (stream to stdout, NO `-o`) — scurl classifies that as **text** and pipes the tarball through `mask_filter` (`sed -u`), **corrupting the binary stream**. (1) Fix classification: NEVER run `mask_filter` on a body destined for a pipe/download — only mask human-facing text (e.g. gate masking on stdout being a TTY, or drop mask_filter for any non-`-o` streamed body). (2) Harden the naive parser: it takes the FIRST `https?://` arg as the URL and misses `--output=FILE`, `--url X`, and mis-detects a `-H` header value that looks like a URL. (3) Add `automation/lib/test_masking.sh`: asserts a piped binary body is byte-identical (no sed mangling), a github URL gets the auth header AND the token is masked in TEXT output, and `--output=` is detected.
**Where:** `automation/lib/masking.sh`, new `automation/lib/test_masking.sh`, wire into the shell-test/lint gate.
**Done When:** `curl … | tar` through scurl is byte-identical to raw curl; parser handles the 3 edge cases; test green; `just drift-gate` green.

## AGY-98  (WS-HARDEN / empty-env contract, **P1**) — one shared empty-`MIOS_*` strip + an import-clean-under-empty-env test
**Who:** you (Python). **When:** independent.
**What + How:** the SSOT var-closure (`usr/lib/mios/userenv.sh:~598`) exports ~734 `MIOS_*` keys, many **empty** (var-closure). An **empty** value (vs ABSENT) defeats `os.environ.get(K, D)` — the default only applies when absent — so int/float coercion `ValueError`s crashed the 56-test gate. Claude patched TWO ad-hoc spots: `mios_pipe/__init__._strip_empty_mios_env()` + a `{ unset $(compgen -v MIOS_); … }` wrapper in `automation/build.sh`. Consolidate: (1) one helper `usr/lib/mios/mios_env.py::strip_empty_mios_env(env=os.environ)` used by `mios_pipe/__init__.py` (drop the private copy); (2) a `test_mios_env.py` that sets EVERY closure-emitted `MIOS_*` key to `""` and asserts every `agent-pipe/mios_*.py` module still imports + its config-coercion falls back to defaults (no `ValueError`); (3) evaluate making the closure NOT emit purely-empty keys at all (ties to the unified-key-library / AGY-84) — if safe, that's the ROOT fix and the strip becomes belt-and-suspenders.
**Where:** new `usr/lib/mios/mios_env.py`, `usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/__init__.py`, new `test_mios_env.py`, (optionally) `usr/lib/mios/userenv.sh`.
**Done When:** one strip helper (no duplicate); the empty-env import test is green across all agent-pipe modules; `just drift-gate` green.

- Where clause 'cross-ref the kickstart path (CATREPO-01)' not done — script has no reference to or cross-link with the kickstart path.
- Scope leak: the commit's referenced_names.txt hunk adds MIOS_MINI_ENABLED (MiOS-Mini split-plane), unrelated to the installer.
- Correctness concern (secondary, unverifiable offline): line 71 invokes `bootc install to-disk --transport oci-archive "$TARGET_DISK" "$OCI_ARCHIVE"` passing BOTH disk and archive as positionals; real `bootc install to-disk` takes a single DEVICE positional with source via `--source-imgref oci-archive:/path`, so this form would likely fail on a live run — though it mirrors the spec's loose `--transport oci` wording.

### AGY-120  [BROKEN]  (e6c1e07d)
- Tests never invoke the real gates: automation/tests/test-drift-gates.sh has 0 references to 38-drift-checks.sh and never calls check_curl_retry/check_nested_podman_caps/check_bake_budget. The tests touch none of these — they assert on inline literals.
- Gate 66 test does not even mirror the real check's logic: it compares hardcoded projected_gb=45 > budget_gb=40 (a GB projection), but check_bake_budget actually counts SBOM sidecar rows > 30. The reimplementation is wrong as well as detached.
- Vacuous pass: the harness exits 0 unconditionally and would pass identically if checks 64/65/66 were deleted or broken — it proves nothing about the safety nets. No 'passes on HEAD' assertion against the real gate either.

## AGY-123  (WS-ORCH, **P1**) — Pure pre-execution validator for the runtime agent DAG
**Who:** you (Python, agent-pipe). **What+How:** routing/dag_exec.py (1585 ln) only handles a malformed plan REACTIVELY at runtime -- line ~918 'nothing ready + nothing running -> cycle/dangling dep: force one' -- so a cycle, self-loop, dangling dependency, or duplicate node id burns a whole fan-out before the nondeterministic 'force one' recovery kicks in. Add a pure sibling dag_validate.py that runs Kahn topological classification (acyclic | cycle-nodes | dangling-deps | duplicate-ids | orphan-roots) over the plan node list BEFORE scheduling; dag_exec calls it and on invalid degrades to a deterministic linearization / single-agent instead of live improvisation. Pure stdlib, never imports server.
**Where:** new usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/routing/dag_validate.py; usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/test_mios_dag_validate.py; call-site edit in usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/routing/dag_exec.py. **Done When:** dag_validate is invoked pre-schedule and returns a typed verdict; test_mios_dag_validate.py green with negative cases for cycle, self-loop, dangling dep and duplicate id; drift checks 6 (server-free import) + 11 (sibling test) pass; just drift-gate green

**Where:** tests/test-bake-group.sh (new), usr/libexec/mios/mios-bake-group, Justfile (drift-gate target), automation/tests/. **Done When:** `bash tests/test-bake-group.sh` passes all three cases against the stub podman; the retry-count log message matches the actual loop bound; the test runs inside `just drift-gate`; `bash -n` clean on both files; `just drift-gate` green.

## AGY-148  (WS-GATE, **P2**) — Fail-closed on absent tooling (MIOS_DRIFT_REQUIRE_TOOLS) to kill the vacuous-pass class
**Who:** you (bash). **What+How:** 38-drift-checks.sh contains ~163 return-0/skip paths and its own header admits checks 'Vacuous-passes where python3 or the copies are absent' — so on a runner without python3 the security gates silently PASS. Set MIOS_DRIFT_REQUIRE_TOOLS=1 in both CI workflows (where python3 is guaranteed) so CI can never false-green a critical check.
**Where:** automation/38-drift-checks.sh, .github/workflows/mios-ci.yml, .forgejo/workflows/build-mios.yml. **Done When:** with python3 hidden from PATH and MIOS_DRIFT_REQUIRE_TOOLS=1, a critical check exits 1 (fail-closed); with the flag unset it still exits 0 (byte-identical to today); CI sets the flag; a negatives-harness case proves both modes; `just drift-gate` green on HEAD.

## AGY-182  (WS-VECTOR, **P1**) — AGY-123 — normalize HNSW index params + emb_version widths across the emb schema + drift-check (vector-schema hygiene)
**Who:** you (SQL + bash/awk drift-gate). **What+How:** schema-init.sql is inconsistent: the 4 original vector indexes (knowledge:42, agent_memory:72, mios_rag:452, config_kv:567) carry the canonical `WITH (m = 16, ef_construction = 64)`, but the ~19 newer HNSW indexes added by AGY-7/11/18/22 (skill/verb/tool_call/directory_entry:635-638, package_set..preset:654-776, event/session:783-788, account_preference:819) OMIT the params and silently ride pgvector defaults, contradicting the AGY-3/7/11 'mirror the exact DDL' rule; `mios_identity.account_preferences.emb` (1139) has NO index at all and a mismatched `emb_version varchar(32)` vs the varchar(64) used everywhere else. ## AGY-184  (WS-VECTOR, **P2**) — AGY-125 — reconcile the duplicate account-preference tables + fix allocate_gid() UPG collision
**Who:** you (SQL + Python). **What+How:** Two competing preference tables exist: `account_preference` (public, AGY-22 line 809 — layer-based, HNSW-indexed, emb_model+emb_version, and the ONLY one read, by materialize-user-config.py:87) versus the dead `mios_identity.account_preferences` (T-246, line 1134 — UUID/pref_key, NO reader or writer anywhere, NO HNSW index, NO emb_model, mismatched emb_version varchar(32)). Reconcile to ONE canonical surface: either drop the dead T-246 table or replace it with a compatibility VIEW onto account_preference — document which and why. Also fix `allocate_gid()` (lines 803-807) which draws from the SAME `uid_alloc` sequence as `allocate_uid()`, making uid==gid user-private-group impossible (a fresh user gets uid=1000, gid=1001); give gid its own sequence OR make allocate_gid mirror the uid for UPG. Add a drift-check asserting exactly one preferences table and no shared alloc sequence.
**Where:** usr/share/mios/postgres/schema-init.sql, usr/libexec/mios/materialize-user-config.py, usr/libexec/mios/seed-db-config.py, automation/38-drift-checks.sh, usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/test_mios_account_sync.py. **Done When:** schema applies idempotently; only one preference surface remains (verified by the new gate, which goes RED if a second `*account_preference*` table reappears); allocate_uid/allocate_gid yield a UPG-consistent pair asserted in a test; materialize-user-config still round-trips a seeded pref; `just drift-gate` passes.

## AGY-192  (WS-SEC, **P1**) — Harden redact.py: expand secret patterns + recurse structured payloads

Extends AGY-8, distinct from AGY-32/33.
**Where:** usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/redact.py, usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/test_mios_redact.py, call sites in usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/federation/a2a.py + mios_pipe/memory/*. **Done When:** test_mios_redact.py gains cases for each new pattern (PEM/JWT/glpat/xox/AKIA/generic assignment) plus a nested-dict case where a secret under a benign scope is masked, and a negative case (benign text unchanged); all redact tests green under `just drift-gate`.

Add a new drift-check (next free number, 69) in `automation/38-drift-checks.sh` that extracts the target set from all four surfaces (parse the `.sh` dispatch `case` arms, the `.sh` usage() heredoc, the `.ps1` catalog keys, and the README grammar list + mapping-table rows) using the SAME multi-path `../mios-bootstrap` resolver the kickstart/ventoy checks already use (lines 3320-3348, degrade-open when the repo is absent) and FAIL on any mismatch. Then FIX the drift so the gate is green: complete `usage()` and add the README mapping-table rows, and either add Linux dispatch arms for monitor/repos or record them in one in-file SSOT list of Windows-only-guidance targets so the sets reconcile.
**Where:** installation/mios-install.sh, installation/README.md, automation/38-drift-checks.sh (new check 69). **Done When:** the new check parses all 4 surfaces and passes at HEAD after the usage/README fixes; a negative fixture (delete one target from usage()) makes the check exit non-zero; `bash -n installation/mios-install.sh` clean; `just drift-gate` green.

## AGY-222  (WS-INSTALL, **P1**) — SSOT-project the Linux target-prereq catalog (kill hardcoded git/curl/podman) + wire rust + show in --dry-run
**Who:** you (bash + TOML). **What+How:** `resolve_target_prereqs()` in `installation/mios-install.sh` (line 416) HARDCODES `for pkg in git curl podman` instead of resolving from SSOT, never ensures the Rust toolchain that native/build targets need (mios-common.sh already ships `mios_ensure_rust`, line 118, but nothing calls it), and runs at line 473 — AFTER the `--dry-run` early-exit at line 456 — so a dry-run never reveals what it would install. Add a `[install.prereqs.<target>]` (or a linux sub-table under the existing `[bootstrap.prereqs]`, mios.toml:8893) SSOT block enumerating the dnf packages per target; make `resolve_target_prereqs` read it via `mios_ssot_value`; call `mios_ensure_rust` for build/update/native targets; and move the prereq PLAN print into the `--dry-run` block so the dry-run shows the resolved package list + rust decision without executing (still exit 0). Add a `test_mios_install_prereqs.sh` asserting `--dry-run` prints the SSOT-resolved list for each target and that no literal `git curl podman` package list remains in the script.
**Where:** installation/mios-install.sh, installation/mios-common.sh, usr/share/mios/mios.toml ([install.prereqs.*]), new installation/test_mios_install_prereqs.sh. **Done When:** prereqs resolve from SSOT (grep proves no hardcoded pkg list); `--dry-run` for every target prints the resolved prereq plan + exits 0 with no side effects; the test is green; `bash -n` clean; `just drift-gate` green.

## AGY-223  (WS-INSTALL, **P1**) — harden mios_ensure_repo fetch to the bootstrap.sh gold pattern (curl --retry + Forgejo fallback + body-validate) + coverage gate
**Who:** you (bash + drift-check). **What+How:** `mios_ensure_repo` in `installation/mios-common.sh` (line 107) fetches the bootstrap tarball with a bare `curl -fsSL ... | tar` — NO `--retry`, no `--max-time`, no downloaded-body validation, and GitHub-only — while the sibling `bootstrap.sh` already implements the correct hardened pattern (`--retry 3 --retry-delay 2 --retry-connrefused --max-time 120`, `-s` non-empty check, cache-bust). This violates the spirit of the AGY-96 curl-retry gate (check 64), which does not currently scan `installation/*.sh`. Bring `mios_ensure_repo` up to the gold pattern AND add a Forgejo mirror fallback (GitHub and Forgejo are equal publishers per the release-topology memory), resolving org/repo/mirror hosts from SSOT (`[bootstrap]`, mios.toml:8710) rather than the literal `github.com`. Then extend the coverage: add a small drift-check (or widen check 64's file glob via the multi-path `../mios-bootstrap` resolver) asserting every network fetch in `installation/*.sh` carries `--retry`/`--tries`.
**Where:** installation/mios-common.sh, automation/38-drift-checks.sh (extend/adjacent to check 64), new installation/test_mios_common_fetch.sh (mock curl). **Done When:** mios_ensure_repo carries --retry/--max-time + body-check + a Forgejo fallback resolved from SSOT; the gate flags a retry-less fetch in installation/*.sh and passes at HEAD; the mock-curl test proves the fallback path fires when the primary host fails; `bash -n` clean; `just drift-gate` green.

## AGY-224  (WS-TEST, **P2**) — test_mios_common.sh — unit-cover the awk SSOT resolver + wire a shell-test gate
**Who:** you (bash). **What+How:** `mios_ssot_value` in `installation/mios-common.sh` (lines 26-45) is the single most load-bearing shared contract (every installer surface resolves ports/colors through it) yet has ZERO tests. Its awk is subtle: it must return a quoted value even when it contains `#` (the hex-color case, line 35), strip an inline `# comment` from an unquoted value (line 37), honor layer precedence user>host>vendor (`mios_ssot_layers`, lines 14-24), fall back to the DEFAULT arg on a missing key, and never break callers under `set -o pipefail`. Write `installation/test_mios_common.sh` with fixtures for each of these behaviors (including a `#1A407F`-style value and a value with a trailing inline comment), and wire it into a shell-test gate mirroring the existing `automation/test_generate-sbom.sh` + its gate.
**Where:** new installation/test_mios_common.sh, automation/38-drift-checks.sh (shell-test wiring). **Done When:** the test passes at HEAD; deliberately deleting the quoted-value awk branch (line 35) makes the hex-color case FAIL; the test is invoked by the shell-test gate; `bash -n` clean; `just drift-gate` green.

## AGY-225  (WS-CONFIG, **P2**) — cross-language SSOT-resolver value-parity gate (bash mios_ssot_value ≡ pwsh Get-MiosSsotValue)
**Who:** you (bash + Python drift-check). **What+How:** `mios-common.sh:mios_ssot_value` (line 26) and `mios-common.ps1:Get-MiosSsotValue` (line 30) each carry a header comment claiming to mirror the other and `usr/lib/mios/mios_toml.py`, but NOTHING verifies they actually agree on a live `mios.toml`. Degrade-open (skip with a WARN) when pwsh is unavailable, matching the existing platform-gated checks. This locks the two hand-written parsers together so a future edit to one can't silently skew installer behavior across platforms.
**Where:** automation/38-drift-checks.sh (new parity check), fixture key list; reads installation/mios-common.sh + installation/mios-common.ps1 (via the ../mios-bootstrap multi-path resolver). **Done When:** the parity check runs both resolvers and passes at HEAD; a fixture value the awk would mishandle (hex with `#`) proves the check red when one side regresses; check skips+WARNs (never hard-fails) when pwsh absent; `just drift-gate` green.

## AGY-227  (WS-CONFIG, **P2**) — installer↔Portal /configure route contract gate (prevent a silent 404 for the operator)
**Who:** you (bash + Python drift-check). **What+How:** Both installers open the configurator by URL — `installation/mios-install.sh:resolve_config` builds `http://localhost:<ports.agent_pipe>/configure` (line 378) and `mios-install.ps1` does the same (line 219) — while the actual route is served by `usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/routing/portal.py` at `@portal_router.get("/configure")` (line 1816). **Where:** automation/38-drift-checks.sh (new route-contract check), reads usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/routing/portal.py + installation/mios-install.sh. **Done When:** the check passes at HEAD; a fixture renaming the portal route to `/config2` (or reintroducing a literal port in the installer) makes it red; degrade-open when the bootstrap repo is absent; `just drift-gate` green.

## AGY-240  (WS-OTEL, **P1**) — Dependency-free OTLP/JSON span exporter for the in-memory tracer

## AGY-242  (WS-OTEL, **P1**) — W3C traceparent inbound-adopt + outbound-propagate interop
**Who:** you (Python). **What+How:** observability/trace.py new_trace_id() mints a 16-hex (64-bit) id and server.py (~335-345) propagates a custom `X-MiOS-Trace` header only, so MiOS traces never stitch to a standard W3C-compliant collector or peer. Add W3C Trace Context: widen new_trace_id() to 32-hex (128-bit) keeping new_span_id() at 16-hex, add pure helpers `format_traceparent(trace_id, span_id, sampled)` / `parse_traceparent(header)` (validate `00-<32hex>-<16hex>-<2hex>`), adopt an inbound `traceparent` in server.py's request-mint path, and emit it outbound on the A2A (a2a_client._a2a_send_message_to_peer), MCP (mcp._mcp_http_rpc) and Hermes hops alongside the legacy header.
**Where:** usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/observability/trace.py, usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/server.py, usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/federation/a2a_client.py, mios_pipe/federation/mcp.py, test_mios_trace.py. **Done When:** test_mios_trace.py asserts parse(format(id,span,True)) round-trips, rejects a malformed traceparent, and confirms new_trace_id() is 32-hex; a test drives an outbound call stub and asserts a valid `traceparent` header is set; existing trace tests still pass; `just drift-gate` green.

## AGY-244  (WS-FED, **P1**) — Enforce AgentCard signature verification on peer probe
**Who:** you (Python). **What+How:** a2a_client._a2a_fetch_card / _a2a_probe_peer fetch a peer's AgentCard and index its skills WITHOUT ever calling a2a.py's `_verify_agent_card_signature`, so a signed card's issuer is never checked and a forged card is trusted blindly. Wire verification into the probe behind a NEW [a2a].require_signed_cards SSOT flag: when set, an invalid signature makes the probe reject (status 'card-signature-invalid') and record a reputation demerit via the injected _A2A_REPUTATION; unsigned cards and flag-off stay fail-open (unchanged behavior). ## AGY-247  (WS-MCP, **P1**) — MCP tools/list pagination (cursor) correctness
**Who:** you (Python). **What+How:** mcp._mcp_probe_server (line ~490) calls `tools/list` exactly once (rid=2), reads `result.tools`, and IGNORES `result.nextCursor` — per the MCP spec a server with more tools than one page returns a cursor, so MiOS silently registers only page 1 and drops the rest. Replace the single call with a bounded cursor loop (pass `params={'cursor': nextCursor}` until absent or a max-page cap), accumulating tools before the allowed_tools filter + registry write; mirror the same fix in the stdio path (_mcp_probe_stdio). Keep fail-open per server.
**Where:** usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/mios_pipe/federation/mcp.py, usr/lib/mios/agent-pipe/test_mios_mcp.py. **Done When:** test_mios_mcp.py stubs a fake RPC returning two pages (page 1 with nextCursor, page 2 without) and asserts ALL tools from both pages register under mcp.<sid>.<tool>, and a page cap prevents an infinite loop; `just drift-gate` green.

### Reporting back
Commit each task as `agy: <task-id> <summary>` and push to `main`. Claude is monitoring
`main` for your commits + will integrate/verify. If blocked, leave a `TODO(agy):` note in
the file and move to the next task. Full context for every item is in `TASKS.md`
(T-166, T-178, T-242, T-165) and the `usr/share/doc/mios/reference/*.md` workstream docs.
